I want to make this review for future guest to know if you want to rent a month and its the middle of the month of lets say june go somewhere else since they'll make you pay the whole month for just 2 weeks of service. This is sad and i feel robbed honestly never experienced this with any other storage unit. I have one in medera California one in Albuquerque new Mexico one in Indianapolis Indiana and none of them have done this. GO SOMEWHERE ELSE SAVE YOUR MONEY!!!<//Review>

<Review>I've been here a couple of times from the first week they've opened to the present. I'm happy that the quality and flavor has gone up.

I usually get rice with two scoops of salmon, ponzu sauce, and a bunch of the toppings. Mango and avocado are a $1 extra, unsurprisingly. Because my office isn't far, I would just buy an avocado from The Market and slice it myself.

You can build your own bowl, or you can order one of their pre-made ones. The line gets pretty long during the lunch hour, and it can seem hectic putting in your order. And if you're short like me, it can be hard to hear and speak to the employees as the sneeze guard is very tall.  But the line does go fast.

If your base is mixed greens, ask for more of the sauce. The greens are not dressed, so all the moisture will be coming from the fish.

Unfortunately, the last time I ate here, there was a piece of plastic in my poke bowl.  I was really hungry, and luckily I wasn't inhaling my food because I would've swallowed it, and it was really sharp.  I thought it might've been a fish bone, but after further inspection, it definitely was plastic.  I didn't want to walk back there from my office, so I e-mailed corporate, but I never got a response.

I really like the poke here, but I don't want to risk eating a sharp piece of plastic.</Review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOo5S9ZdAB2H4VabY-1r-xlNQjfjowfJfLp4pje=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics><response>None< /response>< Gmap_id>

< review>
This Metro PCS store is one of the better ones. The employees are very friendly and courteous and as well as very very knowledgeable about their products and they know what is wrong with your phone and how to fix it when you bring it in for problem.
But if they aren't able to fix it they can send it in to be repaired but you would also have to pay a fee for that, especially if you don't have insurance for the phone and I suggest getting insurance for your cell phone because that is the best decision and add-on that you can get for your phone as they can replace it with a new one of the same type and if they don't have the same phone they give you a new one just as good if not better.
You can pay your bill outside on an ATM like machine when they are closed at any time of the day or night.
The only downfall is they can be out of stock on a lot of the better phones. So unless you don't mind waiting, then you can wait until a new stock/shipment comes in with that phone or they can/will order you one.
That store is considered a MetroPCS corporate store so they are able to do much more than just pay your bill and set up a new line.
I like going to this MetroPCS store than any of the other ones. I only go to the other Metro Stores if there's a phone I really really want and it's not in stock at this one. So really, why go to other Metro PCS stores? Unless it's just to pay a bill and it's close to your house, then I can understand why.
Oh, and they do tend to get pretty busy at times which results in a wait time, but that should show that they are good and know what they are doing and worth the wait.<//review>

From the moment of walking into the office, Ms. Cynthia,the young lady who helped my girlfriend and I, was very courtesy and professional. When we asked about the availability and sizes of their storage units, she immediately asked what sizes, and what amount of space we will need. After giving her our specifics on what we were going to store, she took us to view 2 of their bigger units so we can get a clear view of what we can choose from.

Used to eat here a long time ago, but had to put them on the no fly list cause they kept getting orders wrong. Thought I'd give them another chance today cause my daughter suggested it. Thought they might have fixed the problem. But no! Went through drive thru. What a train wreck! Cars stacked up everywhere after the drive thru waiting for their orders. Employees running around in a panic (seriously) trying to find which order goes where. My order visited 3 other cars before I got it. AND THEY GOT MY ORDER WRONG AGAIN!!! They forgot my daughter's entree. We had to flag down the poor girl who was desparetly trying to match orders with cars. She said, "okay, I'll bring it right out."  Nope. We saw her continuing to literally run around to match up other people's orders. She forgot about us. I don't fault her. She was beyond stressed. We never got the rest of the order. This store is so badly managed and the extra drive thru business during the pandemic didn't force them to fix what was broken. They are apparently happy running a broken business. UNLESS YOU ENJOY DISAPPOINTMENT, STAY AWAY FROM THIS STORE! STAY FAR AWAY!!!!! McDonalds used to be the fast food industry standard of excellence. This will be the last time I go here. I don't like to have to walk through the gross mini-mart to get to the restaurant.  The place inside was filthy.
